        <div class="js-tweet-text-container">
  <p class="TweetTextSize TweetTextSize--normal js-tweet-text tweet-text" lang="en" data-aria-label-part="0">We are thrilled to have nearly 70 events taking place this year at <a href="/hashtag/WalesWeekLondon?src=hash" data-query-source="hashtag_click" class="twitter-hashtag pretty-link js-nav" dir="ltr"><s>#</s><b>WalesWeekLondon</b></a> from February 24th - March 10th. Have you had an opportunity to see whats going on yet? Take a look here: 

<a href="https://t.co/q1jhLUAUHb" rel="nofollow noopener" dir="ltr" data-expanded-url="https://walesweek.london/whats-on" class="twitter-timeline-link" target="_blank" title="https://walesweek.london/whats-on"><span class="tco-ellipsis"></span><span class="invisible">https://</span><span class="js-display-url">walesweek.london/whats-on</span><span class="invisible"></span><span class="tco-ellipsis"><span class="invisible"></span></span></a>

It seems <a href="/PhilipHammondUK" class="twitter-atreply pretty-link js-nav" dir="ltr" data-mentioned-user-id="2653613168"><s>@</s><b>PhilipHammondUK</b></a> will stick to water <a href="/hashtag/Budget2017?src=hash" data-query-source="hashtag_click" class="twitter-hashtag pretty-link js-nav" dir="ltr"><s>#</s><b>Budget2017</b></a></p>
